When a request arrives with an API key (via Bearer token or Basic auth with 'api_key' username), the `Authenticate()` method is invoked.\\n\\nThe authentication flow begins in `pkg/services/authn/authnimpl/registration.go` where `ProvideRegistration()` registers the API key client with the authentication service. For new tokens, it uses `satokengen.Decode()` from `pkg/components/satokengen/tokengen.go` which validates the checksum and extracts the secret. For legacy keys, it uses `apikeygen.Decode()` from `pkg/components/apikeygen/apikeygen.go`. Both decode methods call `GetAPIKeyByHash()` in `pkg/services/apikey/apikeyimpl/xorm_store.go` to retrieve the key from the database.\\n\\n3. **Scope and Security Validation** (`api_key.go` lines 212-231): The `validateApiKey()` function enforces scope enforcement and security checks:\\n   - **Expiration Check**: Validates that `key.Expires` (if set) is greater than the current Unix timestamp\\n   - **Revocation Check**: Ensures `key.IsRevoked` is not true\\n   - **Organization Enforcement**: Verifies the API key's `OrgID` matches the requested organization (scope enforcement)\\n   - **Service Account Requirement**: Ensures the key is associated with a valid service account (`ServiceAccountId >= 1`)\\n\\n4. **Identity Creation**: Upon successful validation, `newServiceAccountIdentity()` creates a service account identity with `SyncPermissions: true` to fetch and enforce the service account's permissions.\\n\\n5. **Last Used Tracking** (`api_key.go` lines 158-245): The `Hook()` method implements the `HookClient` interface to update the API key's `LastUsedAt` timestamp in the database via `UpdateAPIKeyLastUsedDate()`. The `shouldUpdateLastUsedAt()` function prevents excessive updates by only updating if the last usage was more than 5 minutes ago.\\n\\nThe API key model is defined in `pkg/services/apikey/model.go` with critical security fields:\\n- `Expires`: Nullable int64 Unix timestamp for expiration\\n- `IsRevoked`: Nullable boolean flag for revocation status  \\n- `LastUsedAt`: Nullable DateTime for audit tracking\\n- `ServiceAccountId`: Nullable int64 linking to the service account\\n- `Role`: org.RoleType for the key's role/scope\\n\\nDatabase persistence is managed by `pkg/services/apikey/apikeyimpl/xorm_store.go`, which implements the `store` interface with methods for key retrieval (`GetAPIKeyByHash`, `GetApiKeyByName`), creation (`AddAPIKey` with expiration handling), and auditing (`UpdateAPIKeyLastUsedDate`).
